\doxysection{list.\+h}
\hypertarget{_e_a_s_t_l_2include_2_e_a_s_t_l_2list_8h_source}{}\label{_e_a_s_t_l_2include_2_e_a_s_t_l_2list_8h_source}\index{runtime/EASTL/include/EASTL/list.h@{runtime/EASTL/include/EASTL/list.h}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copyright\ (c)\ Electronic\ Arts\ Inc.\ All\ rights\ reserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ file\ implements\ a\ doubly-\/linked\ list,\ much\ like\ the\ C++\ std::list\ class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ primary\ distinctions\ between\ this\ list\ and\ std::list\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ doesn't\ implement\ some\ of\ the\ less-\/frequently\ used\ functions\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ of\ std::list.\ Any\ required\ functions\ can\ be\ added\ at\ a\ later\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ has\ a\ couple\ extension\ functions\ that\ increase\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ can\ contain\ objects\ with\ alignment\ requirements.\ std::list\ cannot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ do\ so\ without\ a\ bit\ of\ tedious\ non-\/portable\ effort.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ has\ optimizations\ that\ don't\ exist\ in\ the\ STL\ implementations\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ supplied\ by\ library\ vendors\ for\ our\ targeted\ platforms.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ supports\ debug\ memory\ naming\ natively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list::size()\ by\ default\ is\ not\ a\ constant\ time\ function,\ like\ the\ list::size\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ in\ some\ std\ implementations\ such\ as\ STLPort\ and\ SGI\ STL\ but\ unlike\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ list\ in\ Dinkumware\ and\ Metrowerks.\ The\ EASTL\_LIST\_SIZE\_CACHE\ option\ can\ change\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ provides\ a\ guaranteed\ portable\ node\ definition\ that\ allows\ users}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ to\ write\ custom\ fixed\ size\ node\ allocators\ that\ are\ portable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ is\ easier\ to\ read,\ debug,\ and\ visualize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ is\ savvy\ to\ an\ environment\ that\ doesn't\ have\ exception\ handling,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ as\ is\ sometimes\ the\ case\ with\ console\ or\ embedded\ environments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ has\ less\ deeply\ nested\ function\ calls\ and\ allows\ the\ user\ to\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ enable\ forced\ inlining\ in\ debug\ builds\ in\ order\ to\ reduce\ bloat.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list\ doesn't\ keep\ a\ member\ size\ variable.\ This\ means\ that\ list\ is\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ smaller\ than\ std::list\ (depends\ on\ std::list)\ and\ that\ for\ most\ operations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ it\ is\ faster\ than\ std::list.\ However,\ the\ list::size\ function\ is\ slower.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ list::size\_type\ is\ defined\ as\ eastl\_size\_t\ instead\ of\ size\_t\ in\ order\ to\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ save\ memory\ and\ run\ faster\ on\ 64\ bit\ systems.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ }
